/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[SP_AttendanceCalculations]    Script Date: 5/15/2024 7:24:57 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Minhaal Azhar>
-- Create date: <16 OCT 2022>
-- Description:	<Calculate attendance by hours of employees by multiple ways>
-- =============================================
create PROCEDURE [dbo].[SP_AttendanceCalculations] --'Employee Wise','1,2','5,6,7','06','2022'

@ReportType VARCHAR(MAX), --'Department Wise'
@DeptId VARCHAR(MAX),
@EmpId VARCHAR(MAX),
@Salary_Month INT,
@Salary_Year INT
AS
BEGIN

IF 1=0 
BEGIN
    SET FMTONLY OFF
END

DECLARE
@employeeAttendanceCount INT,
@counterFetchEmployeeReport INT = 1

DECLARE @tbl_FilteredEmployees TABLE(
Id INT IDENTITY(1,1),
EmployeeId INT NULL,
FirstName VARCHAR(MAX),
LastName VARCHAR(MAX),
DepartmentId INT NULL,
DepartmentName VARCHAR(MAX),
dteJoiningDate DATETIME NULL,
ContractExpiryDate DATETIME NULL,
Active BIT NULL
)
IF OBJECT_ID(N'tempdb..#tempOT') IS NOT NULL
BEGIN
DROP TABLE #tempOT
END


CREATE TABLE #tempOT(
id INT identity(1,1)
,IsPresent BIT
,IsHoliday BIT
,IsPublicHoliday BIT
,AttENDanceId INT NOT NULL
,TimeIn DATETIME
,TimeOut DATETIME
,DailyWorkingHours VARCHAR(MAX)
,WorkingHours INT
,WorkingMinutes INT
,NormalOT INT NULL
,HolidayOT INT NULL
,PublicHolidayOT INT NULL
)

TRUNCATE TABLE tbl_EmployeeAttendanceCalculations

IF(@ReportType = 'Employee Wise')
BEGIN 
INSERT INTO @tbl_FilteredEmployees(EmployeeId,FirstName,LastName,DepartmentId,DepartmentName,dteJoiningDate,ContractExpiryDate,Active) 
										SELECT Id,FirstName,LastName,DepartmentId,(SELECT NAME FROM Departments WHERE Id = h.DepartmentId)DepartmentName,dteJoiningDate,ContractExpiryDate,Active
										FROM HrmEmployees h
										WHERE Active=1 
										AND DepartmentId IN (SELECT VALUE FROM STRING_SPLIT(@DeptId,','))
										AND Id IN (SELECT VALUE FROM STRING_SPLIT(@EmpId,','))
										AND MONTH(dteJoiningDate) <= @Salary_Month 
										AND YEAR(dteJoiningDate) <= @Salary_Year
										AND MONTH(ContractExpiryDate) >= @Salary_Month 
										AND YEAR(ContractExpiryDate) >= @Salary_Year
END
ELSE IF (@ReportType = 'Department Wise')
BEGIN 
INSERT INTO @tbl_FilteredEmployees(EmployeeId,FirstName,LastName,DepartmentId,DepartmentName,dteJoiningDate,ContractExpiryDate,Active) 
										SELECT Id,FirstName,LastName,DepartmentId,(SELECT NAME FROM Departments WHERE Id = h.DepartmentId)DepartmentName,dteJoiningDate,ContractExpiryDate,Active
										FROM HrmEmployees h
										WHERE Active=1 
										AND DepartmentId IN (SELECT VALUE FROM STRING_SPLIT(@DeptId,','))
										AND MONTH(dteJoiningDate) <= @Salary_Month 
										AND YEAR(dteJoiningDate) <= @Salary_Year
										AND MONTH(ContractExpiryDate) >= @Salary_Month 
										AND YEAR(ContractExpiryDate) >= @Salary_Year
END

SET @employeeAttendanceCount = (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM @tbl_FilteredEmployees)

IF(@employeeAttendanceCount > 0)
BEGIN 


WHILE(@employeeAttendanceCount >= @counterFetchEmployeeReport)
BEGIN

DECLARE
@_deptId INT = (SELECT DepartmentId FROM  @tbl_FilteredEmployees WHERE Id = @counterFetchEmployeeReport),
@_empId INT = (SELECT EmployeeId FROM  @tbl_FilteredEmployees WHERE Id = @counterFetchEmployeeReport)

-------------------------------------------------@NAME (START)---------------------------------------------------


DECLARE @Name VARCHAR(MAX)				=	(SELECT CONCAT(FirstName,' ',LastName) FROM @tbl_FilteredEmployees WHERE Id = @counterFetchEmployeeReport)


-------------------------------------------------@NAME (END)-----------------------------------------------------

-------------------------------------------------@DepartmentName (START)-----------------------------------------


DECLARE @DepartmentName VARCHAR(MAX)	=	(SELECT DepartmentName FROM @tbl_FilteredEmployees WHERE Id = @counterFetchEmployeeReport)


-------------------------------------------------@DepartmentName (END)-------------------------------------------

-------------------------------------------------@PresentDays (START)-----------------------------------------


DECLARE @PresentDays INT				=	(SELECT COUNT(*) 
															FROM AttENDances
															WHERE EmployeeId = @_empId
															AND Department = @_deptId
															AND MONTH(Date) = @Salary_Month
															AND YEAR(Date) = @Salary_Year
															AND ISNULL(IsPresent,0)=1),

-------------------------------------------------@PresentDays (END)-------------------------------------------

-------------------------------------------------@LeaveDays (START)-------------------------------------------


	@LeaveDays INT					=	(SELECT COUNT(*)
															FROM AttENDances
															WHERE EmployeeId = @_empId
															AND Department = @_deptId
															AND MONTH(Date) = @Salary_Month
															AND YEAR(Date) = @Salary_Year
															AND ISNULL(IsLeave,0)=1),


-------------------------------------------------@LeaveDays (END)-------------------------------------------

-------------------------------------------------@AbsentDays (START)-------------------------------------------


	@AbsentDays INT					=	(SELECT COUNT(*)
															FROM AttENDances
															WHERE EmployeeId = @_empId
															AND Department = @_deptId
															AND MONTH(Date) = @Salary_Month
															AND YEAR(Date) = @Salary_Year
															AND ISNULL(IsLeave,0)=1)

															
-------------------------------------------------@AbsentDays (END)-------------------------------------------


-------------------------------------------------@NormalOT (START)-------------------------------------------

TRUNCATE TABLE #tempOT

INSERT INTO #tempOT
		(
		AttENDanceId
		,IsPresent
		,IsHoliday
		,IsPublicHoliday
		,TimeIn
		,TimeOut
		,DailyWorkingHours
		,WorkingHours
		,WorkingMinutes
		,NormalOT
		,HolidayOT
		,PublicHolidayOT
		)
SELECT 
		AttendaceId
		,IsPresent
		,IsHoliday
		,IsPublicHoliday
		,TimeIn
		,TimeOut
		,CONVERT(VARCHAR(2), DATEDIFF(MINUTE, TimeIn , TimeOut) / 60)  + ':' +  RIGHT('0' + CONVERT(VARCHAR(2), DATEDIFF(MINUTE, TimeIn , TimeOut) % 60), 2)
		,CAST(CONVERT(VARCHAR(2), DATEDIFF(MINUTE, TimeIn , TimeOut) / 60) AS INT)
		,CAST(RIGHT('0' + CONVERT(VARCHAR(2), DATEDIFF(MINUTE, TimeIn , TimeOut) % 60), 2) AS INT)
		,NULL
		,NULL
		,NULL
		FROM AttENDances
		WHERE EmployeeId = @_empId
		AND Department = @_deptId
		AND MONTH(Date) = @Salary_Month
		AND YEAR(Date) = @Salary_Year
		AND (ISNULL(IsPresent,0)=1 OR (ISNULL(IsHoliday,0)=1 AND TimeIn IS NOT NULL AND TimeOut IS NOT NULL))
		
DECLARE @str VARCHAR(MAX),
@HolidayOrWorkingDay VARCHAR(MAX)
DECLARE @count INT = 1,
@maxCount INT = (SELECT count(*) FROM #tempOT),
@WorkingHours INT, 
@WorkingMinutes INT,
@NormalOT INT = 0,
@HolidayOT INT = 0,
@PublicHolidayOT INT = 0,
@counter INT = 1

WHILE(@maxCount >= @count)
BEGIN

SET @NormalOT = 0;
SET @HolidayOT = 0;
SET @PublicHolidayOT = 0;
SET @WorkingHours			= (SELECT WorkingHours FROM #tempOT WHERE id = @count)
SET @WorkingMinutes			= (SELECT WorkingMinutes FROM #tempOT WHERE id = @count)
SET @HolidayOrWorkingDay	= (SELECT (CASE WHEN IsPresent = 1 THEN 'Working Day'
											WHEN IsHoliday = 1 THEN 'Holiday'
											WHEN IsPublicHoliday = 1 THEN 'Public Holiday'
											ELSE '' END) 
											FROM #tempOT WHERE id = @count)

	IF(@HolidayOrWorkingDay = 'Working Day')
	BEGIN
--------------------------------------------HOUR == 9 && MIN >=45------------------------------------

		IF(@WorkingHours = 9 and @WorkingMinutes >=45)
		BEGIN
		SET @NormalOT = @NormalOT+1
		END


--------------------------------------------HOUR > 9------------------------------------

		ELSE IF (@WorkingHours > 9)
		BEGIN
		DECLARE @a INT = @WorkingHours - 9;
		DECLARE @b INT = @a * 60;
		DECLARE @c INT = @WorkingMinutes + @b;
		DECLARE @d decimal = ceiling(cast(@c as decimal(7,2))/60)
		SET @counter = 1;
	
			WHILE(@d >= @counter)
			BEGIN
			SET @counter = @counter + 1;
	
				IF(@c >= 45)
				BEGIN
				SET @NormalOT = @NormalOT + 1;
				SET @c = @c - 60;
				END
	
			END
		END
		UPDATE #tempOT SET NormalOT = @NormalOT WHERE id = @count
	END
	
	ELSE IF(@HolidayOrWorkingDay = 'Holiday')
	BEGIN
		DECLARE @totalMinutesWorkingHoliday  INT = (@WorkingHours * 60) + @WorkingMinutes
		DECLARE @expectedHolidayCounter INT = CEILING(CAST(@totalMinutesWorkingHoliday AS DECIMAL(7,2))/60)
		SET @counter = 1
		WHILE(@expectedHolidayCounter>=@counter)
		BEGIN
		SET @counter = @counter + 1
			IF(@totalMinutesWorkingHoliday>=60)
			BEGIN
			SET @HolidayOT = @HolidayOT + 1
			SET @totalMinutesWorkingHoliday = @totalMinutesWorkingHoliday - 60
			END
		END
	UPDATE #tempOT SET HolidayOT = @HolidayOT WHERE id = @count
	END

	ELSE IF(@HolidayOrWorkingDay = 'Public Holiday')
	BEGIN
		DECLARE @totalMinutesWorkingPublicHoliday  INT = (@WorkingHours * 60) + @WorkingMinutes
		DECLARE @expectedPublicHolidayCounter INT = CEILING(CAST(@totalMinutesWorkingPublicHoliday AS DECIMAL(7,2))/60)
		SET @counter = 1
		WHILE(@expectedPublicHolidayCounter>=@counter)
		BEGIN
		SET @counter = @counter + 1
			IF(@totalMinutesWorkingPublicHoliday>=60)
			BEGIN
			SET @PublicHolidayOT = @PublicHolidayOT + 1
			SET @totalMinutesWorkingPublicHoliday = @totalMinutesWorkingPublicHoliday - 60
			END
		END
	UPDATE #tempOT SET PublicHolidayOT = @PublicHolidayOT WHERE id = @count
	END
SET @count = @count + 1
END

DECLARE @NormalOTHours INT = (SELECT SUM(NormalOT) FROM #tempOT),
		@HolidayOTHours INT = (SELECT SUM(HolidayOT) FROM #tempOT),
		@PublicHolidayOTHours INT = (SELECT SUM(PublicHolidayOT) FROM #tempOT)
-------------------------------------------------@NormalOT (END)-------------------------------------------

-------------------------------------------------@TotalHoursWorked (START)-------------------------------------------


		IF OBJECT_ID(N'tempdb..#tempDailyWorkedHours') IS NOT NULL
		BEGIN
		DROP TABLE #tempDailyWorkedHours
		END

			SELECT 
			CONVERT(VARCHAR(2), DATEDIFF(MINUTE, TimeIn , TimeOut) / 60) 
			+ ':' + 
			RIGHT('0' + CONVERT(VARCHAR(2), DATEDIFF(MINUTE, TimeIn , TimeOut) % 60), 2)DWH
			INTO #tempDailyWorkedHours
			FROM AttENDances
			WHERE EmployeeId = @_empId
			AND Department = @_deptId
			AND MONTH(Date) = @Salary_Month
			AND YEAR(Date) = @Salary_Year
			AND ISNULL(IsPresent,0)=1
				

DECLARE	@TotalHoursWorked VARCHAR(MAX)			=	(SELECT
				CAST(SUM(DATEDIFF(SECOND,0,DWH))/3600 AS VARCHAR(12)) 
				+ ':' + 
				RIGHT('0' + CAST(SUM(DATEDIFF(SECOND,0,DWH))/60%60 AS VARCHAR(2)),2) 
				FROM #tempDailyWorkedHours)

DECLARE @splitTotalHours VARCHAR(MAX) = CONVERT(VARCHAR(MAX),(SELECT CONVERT(INT, dbo.GetColumnValue(@TotalHoursWorked, ':', 1)) + @NormalOTHours + @HolidayOTHours))
DECLARE @splitTotalMins VARCHAR(MAX) = dbo.GetColumnValue(@TotalHoursWorked, ':', 2)

SET @TotalHoursWorked = @splitTotalHours +':'+@splitTotalMins


-------------------------------------------------@TotalHoursWorked (END)-------------------------------------------

	INSERT INTO tbl_EmployeeAttendanceCalculations
(
	EmployeeId
	,Name
	,Department
	,PresentDays
	,LeaveDays
	,AbsentDays
	,TotalHoursWorked
	,NormalOTHours
	,WeekendOTHours
	,PublicHolidaysOTHours
)
SELECT
	@_empId
	,@Name
	,@DepartmentName
	,@PresentDays
	,@LeaveDays
	,@AbsentDays
	,@TotalHoursWorked
	,@NormalOTHours
	,@HolidayOTHours
	,CASE WHEN @PublicHolidayOTHours IS NULL THEN 0 ELSE @PublicHolidayOTHours END

SET @counterFetchEmployeeReport = @counterFetchEmployeeReport + 1;
END

END
	SELECT * FROM tbl_EmployeeAttendanceCalculations
END
GO
USE [master]
GO
ALTER DATABASE [Talenthrm] SET  READ_WRITE 
GO
